10.1 Tuple-’∂’•÷Ä

‘∏’Ω’ø ’ß’∏÷Ç’©’µ’°’∂ tuple’® ’∂’∏÷Ç’µ’∂ list’∂’°, ’∏÷Ä’´’∂ ’∏÷Ä ’π’´ ’Ø’°÷Ä’•’¨’´ ÷É’∏÷É’∏’≠’•’¨ (immutable ’•’∂)

10.1.1 tuple-’´ ’Ω’ø’•’≤’Æ’∏÷Ç’¥

# ’§’°’ø’°÷Ä’Ø tuple ’Ω’ø’•’≤’Æ’•’¨
tup = ()
# ’Ø’°’¥
tup = tuple()

print(tup)
# ’ß’¨’•’¥’•’∂’ø’∂’•÷Ä’∏’æ tuple ’Ω’ø’•’≤’Æ’•’¨
tup = (1, "’∏’≤’ª’∏÷Ç’µ’∂", True)
tup = 1, "’∏’≤’ª’∏÷Ç’µ’∂", True


print(tup)
# ’•’©’• ’¨’´’Ω’ø ’∏÷Ç’∂’•’∂÷Ñ ’Ø’°÷Ä’°’∂÷Ñ ’§’°÷Ä’±’∂’•’∂÷Ñ ’´÷Ä’°’∂ tuple, ’•÷Ä÷á’´ ’£’∏÷Ç’∑’°’Ø’∏÷Ç’¥ ’•÷Ñ ’©’• ’∏’∂÷Å’ù
lst = [1, "’∏’≤’ª’∏÷Ç’µ’∂", True]
tup = tuple(lst)
print(tup)
# ’•’©’• ’∏÷Ç’¶’∏÷Ç’¥ ’•’∂÷Ñ tuple’´ ’ß’¨’•’¥’•’∂’ø’∂’•÷Ä’® ’¢’°’™’°’∂’•’∂÷Ñ ’ø’°÷Ä’¢’•÷Ä ÷É’∏÷É’∏’≠’°’Ø’°’∂’∂’•÷Ä’´ ’¥’•’ª, ’Ø’°÷Ä’°’∂÷Ñ ’°’∂’•’∂÷Ñ’ù
print(tup)

a, b = 15, 509

a, b, c = tup
print(a, b, c, sep="\n")
tuple(i**2 for i in range(10))




# ’•’©’• ’¶’∏÷Ç’ø (i**2 for i in range(10)) ’£÷Ä’•’∂÷Ñ ’Ø’Ω’°÷Ä÷Ñ’•’∂÷Ñ generator ’Ø’∏’π’æ’∏’≤ ’¢’°’∂, ’∏÷Ä’® ’∞’•’ø’∏ ’•’∂÷Ñ ’°’∂÷Å’∂’•’¨’∏÷Ç

10.1.2 Tuple’´’∂ ’ß’¨’•’¥’•’∂’ø ’°’æ’•’¨’°÷Å’∂’•’¨

tup.append(1)
"asdas"[0] = "A"
# tup.append("’∫’°’∂’´÷Ä")

tup = (15, 508)
print(tup[0])

tup[0] = 12
print(tup)
  • immutable - string, tuple
  • mutable - list
tup[0] = 0 #  TypeError

’≥’°÷Ä’∂’•÷Ä’Ω ’´’∂’π, ’∫’•’ø÷Ñ’° ’∂’∏÷Ä tuple ’Ω’°÷Ä÷Ñ’•’∂÷Ñ

new_tuple = tup + ("’™’°÷Ä’´’ø", 509)
print(new_tuple)

10.1.3 indexing / slicing (’∂’∏÷Ç’µ’∂ ’±÷á ’∏’∂÷Å list’®)

print(new_tuple[1]) # prints: "’∏’≤’ª’∏÷Ç’µ’∂"

print(new_tuple[1:4]) # prints: ('’∏’≤’ª’∏÷Ç’µ’∂', True, '’™’°÷Ä’´’ø')

print(new_tuple[-1]) # Output: 509

10.1.4 ÷Å’´’Ø’¨ ’∫’ø’ø’æ’•’¨’® (’¨÷Ä’´’æ ’∂’∏÷Ç’µ’∂ ’±÷á)

for element in new_tuple:
    print(element)

max((1,2,3))
tuple(i**2 for i in range(10))

10.1.5 ‘±’º’°’æ’•’¨’∏÷Ç’©’µ’∏÷Ç’∂’∂’•÷Ä

  1. tuple-’∂’•÷Ä’´ ’∞’•’ø ’°’æ’•’¨’´ ’°’∫’°’∞’∏’æ’°, ’∏÷Ä’∏’æ’∞’•’ø÷á ’Ø’°÷Ä’°’∂÷Ñ ’æ’Ω’ø’°’∞ ’¨’´’∂’•’∂÷Ñ ’∏÷Ä ’∏’π ’¥’•’Ø ’¥’•÷Ä tuple-’® ’π’´ ÷É’∏’≠’´
  2. ’∞’´’∑’∏’≤’∏÷Ç’©’µ’°’∂ ’ø’•’Ω’°’∂’Ø’µ’∏÷Ç’∂’´÷Å ’°’æ’•’¨’´ ÷Ö’∫’ø’´’¥’°’¨ ’•’∂

10.2 set-’•÷Ä (’¢’°’¶’¥’∏÷Ç’©’µ’∏÷Ç’∂’∂’•÷Ä)

my_set = set() # my_set = {}

print(type(my_set))

# my_set = {}
# print(type(my_set))
my_set = {4, 3, 3, 2}
print(my_set)
my_set = set()

for _ in range(5):
    my_set.add(input()) # append-’´ ÷É’∏’≠’°÷Ä’•’∂ add
    print(my_set)
for i in my_set:
    print(i)
my_set1 = {}
print(type(my_set1)) # ’¶’£’∏÷Ç’µ’∑ ’•’∂÷Ñ ’¨’´’∂’∏÷Ç’¥

10.2.1 ’ß’¨’¥’•’∂’ø ’°’æ’•’¨’°÷Å’∂’•’¨ / ’∞’•’º’°÷Å’∂’•’¨

my_set = {4, 3, 3, 2}
print(my_set)

print(my_set)

# my_set.append()
my_set.add(5) # ’∏’π ’©’• ’£÷Ä’∏÷Ç’¥ ’•’∂÷Ñ my_set = my_set.add(4)
print(my_set)

my_set.remove(3)
print(my_set)
print(my_set.pop())
print(my_set)
for i in my_set:
    print(i)

10.2.2 ‘≤’°’¶’¥’∏÷Ç’©’µ’∏÷Ç’∂’∂’•÷Ä’´ ’∞’•’ø ’£’∏÷Ä’Æ’∏’≤’∏÷Ç’©’µ’∏÷Ç’∂’∂’•÷Ä

set1 = {1, 2, 3, 4}
set2 = {3, 4, 5, 6}

# ’Ñ’´’°’æ’∏÷Ä’∏÷Ç’¥
print(set1.union(set2)) # Output: {1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6}
# ’Ø’°’¥ ’ß’¨
# set1 | set2 (’Ø’°’¥) # caps lock + right shift-’´ ’Ø’∏’≤÷Ñ’® 6

# ’Ä’°’ø’∏÷Ç’¥
print(set1.intersection(set2)) # Output: {3, 4}
# ’Ø’°’¥ ’ß’¨
# set1 & set2 (÷á) # uppercase 6

# ’è’°÷Ä’¢’•÷Ä’∏÷Ç’©’µ’∏÷Ç’∂
print(set1.difference(set2)) # Output: {1, 2}
# ’Ø’°’¥ ’ß’¨
# print(set1 - set2)

# ’ç’´’¥’•’ø÷Ä’´’Ø ’ø’°÷Ä’¢’•÷Ä’∏÷Ç’©’µ’∏÷Ç’∂
print(set1.symmetric_difference(set2)) # Output: {1, 2, 5, 6}
# ’Ø’°’¥ ’ß’¨
# set1 ^ set2 # uppercase 6

10.2.3 Set comparison

a = {1, 2, 3, "a", "b"}
b = {2, 1, 3, "b"}

print(a >= b)

# >, >=, <, <=

10.2.4 ’Ä’•÷Ä’©’°’Ø’°’∂’∏÷Ç’©’µ’∏÷Ç’∂

forum-’∏÷Ç’¥ ÷Ñ’∂’∂’°÷Ä’Ø’∏÷Ç’¥ set-’•÷Ä’´ ’∞’•÷Ä’©’°’Ø’°’∂’∏÷Ç’©’µ’°’∂ ’æ’•÷Ä’°’¢’•÷Ä’µ’°’¨

a = ['’∫’°’∂’´÷Ä', '÷É’´’≤', 11, 12]
print(a)
print(set(a))
set(a)[0]
print(a)
# print(set(a)[0])

print()
print(list(set(a)))
print(list(set(a))[0])
my_set = {1, 4, 4, 3, 2}

for element in my_set:
    print(element)

10.2.5 set comprehension

-5, 6 ’©’æ’•÷Ä’´ ÷Ñ’°’º’°’Ø’∏÷Ç’Ω’´’∂’•÷Ä’´ ’¢’°’¶’¥’∏÷Ç’©’µ’∏÷Ç’∂’® ’Ω’ø’•’≤’Æ’•’¨

lst = []

for i in range(-5, 6):
    lst.append(i**2)
print(lst)

lst = [i**2 for i in range(-5,6)]
print(lst)
s = set() # s = {}

for i in range(-5, 6):
    s.add(i**2)
    # print(s)

print(s)
[] - list
() - tuple
{} - set
s = [i**2 for i in range(-5,6)]
print(s)

s = tuple(i**2 for i in range(-5,6))
print(s)

s = {i**2 for i in range(-5,6)}
print(s)

10.2.6 ‘ø’°÷Ä’°’∂÷Ñ ’∞’°’∂’£’´’Ω’ø in, sum len ‚Ä§‚Ä§ ÷Ö’£’ø’°’£’∏÷Ä’Æ’•’∂÷Ñ

print(s)

print(f"{4 in s = }")
print(f"{len(s) = }")
print(f"{sum(s) = }")

Alice-’®’ù 25 ’ø’°÷Ä’•’Ø’°’∂ ’°, Bob-’®’ù 30, Charlie-’∂ 35: Python-’∏’æ ’∫’°’∞’•÷Ñ ’ß’§ ’´’∂÷Ü’∏÷Ä’¥’°÷Å’´’°’∂

10.3.1 ’Ü’•÷Ä’°’Æ’∏÷Ç’©’µ’∏÷Ç’∂

d = {}
d = dict()

print(type(d))
tariqner = {"Alice": 25, "Bob": 30,
            "Charlie": 35}

print(type(tariqner))
print(tariqner)
print(tariqner["Alice"]) # [0]
# ’Ü’∏÷Ä ’¥’°÷Ä’§ ’°’æ’•’¨’°÷Å’∂’•’¨
tariqner["Dumbledore"] = 40
print(tariqner)
# ÷É’∏÷É’∏’≠’•’¨ ’°÷Ä’™’•÷Ñ’®
tariqner["Dumbledore"] += 1
print(tariqner)
# ’ª’∂’ª’•’¨ ’¥’°÷Ä’§’∏÷Ç
del tariqner["Charlie"] # delete
print(tariqner)
print(tariqner.keys())
print(tariqner.values())
print(tariqner.keys()[0])
print(list(tariqner.keys()))

print(list(tariqner.keys())[0])
tariqner[1] = "12312"
print(tariqner)
tariqner[False] = "Barevner"

print(tariqner)
tariqner[False]
tariqner[3.14] = "pi"
tariqner[[1,2]] = 12312
for mard in tariqner: # ’Ø’°’¥ tariqner.keys()
    print(mard)
for t in tariqner.values():
    print(t)
print(tariqner.items())
for i in tariqner.items():
    print(i, type(i))
    
for i in tariqner.items():
    name, age = i # i[0], i[1]
    print(name, age)
for name, age in tariqner.items():
    print(name, age)

}

11 üõ†Ô∏è ‘≥’∏÷Ä’Æ’∂’°’Ø’°’∂ (ToDo)

11.1 ’Ä’°’∑’æ’•’¨ ’∏÷Ä ’¥÷Ä’£’´÷Å ÷Ñ’°’∂’´ ’∞’°’ø ’Ø’°

mrger = ["apple", "banana", "apple", "orange", "banana", "apple"]
mrger_set = set(mrger)

print(mrger_set, len(mrger_set))
count_dict = {}

for i in mrger_set:
    count_dict[i] = mrger.count(i)    
        
{i:mrger.count(i) for i in mrger_set}
count_dict = {}

for mirg in mrger_set:
    count = 0
    for j in mrger:
        if mirg == j:
            count += 1 
    count_dict[mirg] = count 
    
count_dict   
count_dict = {}

# if len(mrger) == len(set(mrger)):
#     print({i:1 for i in mrger_set})

for mirg in mrger:
    print(mirg, count_dict)

    if mirg not in count_dict:
        count_dict[mirg] = 1
    else:
        count_dict[mirg] += 1
    
    
count_dict   


count_dict = {i:0 for i in mrger_set}

for mirg in mrger:
    count_dict[mirg] += 1
count_dict = {}
print(count_dict)

for mirg in mrger:
    if mirg not in count_dict:
        count_dict[mirg] = 0
    
    count_dict[mirg] += 1   
    print(count_dict)

11.2 Telegram

Settings -> Advanced -> (Scroll down) Export Telegram data -> (Scroll down) Choose ‚ÄúMachine readable JSON‚Äù -> Export

import json 

PATH = "result.json"

with open(PATH, "r") as f:
    data = json.load(f)
chats = data["chats"]["list"]

chats[0]["type"]
types = [i["type"] for i in chats]

count_dict = {i:0 for i in types}

for i in types:
    count_dict[i] += 1
    
count_dict
chats 
count_has_message = 0
chats_not_empty = []

for chat in chats:
    if chat["messages"]:
        count_has_message += 1 
        chats_not_empty.append(chat["name"])

print(f"Perc - {count_has_message / len(chats) * 100:.2f}")
print(chats_not_empty)
chats_list_not_empty = [chat for chat in chats if chat["messages"]]
chats_list_not_empty
